Important Overseas Telegrams

Briand Achieves a Great Victory in the French Parliament 63

Detailed Explanation of Conciliatory Policy

German-Austrian Tariff Treaty Considered of No Political Importance

Eloquent Oratory Enthralls Listeners Like a Narcotic

Public Sentiment Leans Towards Presidential Candidate

National News Agency, Paris, 8th: Today, the French Parliament, following yesterday's grand gathering, saw Foreign Minister Briand provide a detailed explanation of France's foreign policy in recent years, dispelling an atmosphere of suspicion. Briand's hour-long speech showcased his talent for oratory, shifting from vehement to nonchalant, employing his usual skills of manipulation. Although there were occasional jeers from the left and right wings, by the end of Briand's speech, the applause from the entire chamber was thunderous, silencing even his opponents. Following this speech, Briand may soon ascend to the position of head of state. This speech may be Briand's swan song in his active political life. Briand's speech first described the conciliatory policy since the European War. He stated that he knew this policy would encounter many obstacles and opponents, but statesmen such as Tardieu, Laval, and Poincaré deeply believed in it. As for the German-Austrian tariff treaty, Briand has now admitted that the issue is no longer of major importance. The German-Austrian tariff treaty is merely an economic agreement, and although there are regrets to be found, it has no actual political importance. The Germans' mistake was a psychological one, so the French should not be suspicious and cause themselves trouble. Furthermore, he has accepted the suggestion of British Foreign Secretary Henderson to submit the matter to the League of Nations Council for review, so the German-Austrian tariff treaty is like the naval agreement, not yet an established fact. Moreover, France has decided to submit a counterproposal to various countries at the opening of the Pan-European Conference. At that time, the German-Austrian tariff treaty may be completely eliminated by France's counterproposal. Briand concluded by saying that if humanity is determined to maintain peace, where would war come from? He said that he has always striven for peace and will never split with the Germans or harm the relationship between Germany and France.

Reuters, Paris, 8th: Tonight, after a long discussion, the Chamber of Deputies passed a vote of confidence in Briand's foreign policy by 450 votes to 52. Briand stated that Germany made a big mistake in proceeding with the German-Austrian Customs Union. He believes that the solution to economic difficulties lies in the plan for European economic unity, which will be discussed in Geneva. He hopes that the German foreign authorities understand that the era of coercion is now over. Herriot spoke in support of Briand, saying that without an agreement with Britain and the United States, there would be no maritime peace, and without an agreement with Germany, there would be no land peace.

National News Agency, Paris, 8th: After Briand's foreign policy achieved a great victory in Parliament, the radical factions of both the Senate and the Chamber of Deputies decided in a joint meeting with a large majority to send representatives to persuade Briand to run for president. Although Senate President Doumer has rejoined the Radical Party, hoping to share Briand's influence, it is expected that this will still be insufficient to affect the number of votes for the Radical Party. Moreover, Socialist leader Blum also stated in the newspapers that his party supports Briand's candidacy. In addition, several of Briand's political enemies also want him to be elected president so that he can relinquish the position of foreign minister. Therefore, if Briand agrees to run, the presidential seat is almost guaranteed.

Committee of the International Chamber of Commerce Passes China's Proposal 64

Requesting the Convocation of a World Silver Conference

US Representatives Strongly Oppose Cancellation of War Debts

Reuters, Washington, 8th: The International Chamber of Commerce's Proposal Committee has passed the proposal of the Chinese representatives to convene a world conference to handle the silver issue. This proposal can be submitted to the plenary session tomorrow. The proposal states that the International Chamber of Commerce, in view of the serious impact of the current silver market on the world's economic situation, believes that it is necessary to convene a conference this year to hear the opinions of all parties concerned and seek a solution to this difficult problem. It is hoped that the national committees will bring this matter to the attention of their respective governments.

Associated Press, Washington, 8th: Today, there were already a sufficient number of representatives within the International Chamber of Commerce Conference supporting the international silver conference proposal, ensuring its passage. Therefore, attention turned to the war debt issue. European representatives tried to have a resolution for its establishment recorded in the meeting minutes, while US representatives strongly opposed it. Furthermore, Congressman Snell issued a declaration to the International Chamber of Commerce Conference, strongly refuting the cancellation or reduction of war debts, claiming that whenever there is an international gathering, the decision is always to make Americans the sacrificial lamb for their own selfish plans.

Reuters, New York, 8th: The New York Times carried a dispatch from Mexico City, saying that the Mexican financial and industrial circles are greatly delighted by the prospect of the early holding of the World Silver Conference and welcome Washington's advocacy, considering this as a possible method of saving silver prices. Among the general economic decline, one of Mexico's serious burdens is the low price of silver. Recently, Mexico's exchange situation has been very critical, and many silver coins have been withdrawn from the market because there is no possibility of offsetting them with gold.

The Great Danger of a Tuberculosis Family 67

Shared Meals and Tuberculosis

By Yu Yunxiu, a great contemporary Chinese medical scholar

I.

The practice of shared meals is prevalent throughout China, especially in the south. A square table, surrounded by seven or eight people, with various dishes arranged, chopsticks and cups crossing paths. Family members, fathers and sons, gather together in harmony. Hosts and guests, friends and acquaintances, are all satisfied and full. It's certainly warm, intimate, and thoughtful, but it is also a breeding ground for the transmission of disease. To offend this danger is no different from stepping on a sword's edge or walking through fire. Does the reader doubt my words? Please allow me to use tuberculosis as an example. Tuberculosis, even with the advancements of modern medicine, is nearly impossible to cure once the condition has progressed slightly. Once diagnosed, life and death are uncertain. This is something that everyone has heard of and shies away from, avoiding it as quickly as possible. However, it is spreading wider and wider, with more and more people afflicted. We fear it but cannot avoid it, shun it but cannot escape it. Is it truly a matter of fate, hanging by a thread? Or is it a lack of knowledge, poor customs, and the inability to defend against it properly?

II.

Tuberculosis is caused by the transmission of bacteria. It has been over forty years since German doctor Koch discovered the tuberculosis bacillus. Scholars around the world have no objection. This long-standing evil has been exposed, its discovery is no less significant than the Great Yu's cauldron. Today, even women and children know about it, only our old customs remain ignorant. The bacteria is less than fifteen ten-thousandths of a centimeter long and less than five ten-thousandths of a centimeter wide. When viewed under a thousand-fold microscope, it looks like a short mustache. It has no feet, so it cannot walk. It has no tail, so it cannot swim. It has no wings, so it cannot fly. The common belief that tuberculosis is caused by deficiency and exhaustion, and that the "lung worm" is a spiritual creature that escapes from the dying patient and attaches itself to others, is false. Moreover, the "Ziting Extermination of Tuberculosis Formula" even depicts the shape of its six generations. Wang Kentang's "Diagnosis and Treatment Standards" adopted it, but they are all just words of imagined likeness, which is why the Siku Quanshu criticizes it as strange talk.

III.

When the tuberculosis bacteria enter the lungs, they develop, grow, and reproduce. Therefore, the sputum of tuberculosis patients contains many of these bacteria. In severe cases, even a tiny speck of sputum contains thousands of bacteria. This can be seen clearly under a microscope, it is not empty talk. Based on this, the number of bacteria in a single mouthful of sputum is countless, perhaps billions. This sputum, containing billions of bacteria, is spat out from the lungs into the outside world, inevitably passing through the throat, tongue, and lips. Therefore, the amount of sputum containing bacteria that contaminates the patient's throat, tongue, and lips is countless. The number of bacteria clinging to the patient's throat, tongue, and lips is unimaginable. Once cups and chopsticks come into contact with the mouth of a tuberculosis patient, they are contaminated by countless specks of sputum containing bacteria. The number of bacteria clinging to the cups and chopsticks is unimaginable. When a patient uses chopsticks to eat the dishes on the table, the amount of sputum containing bacteria that contaminates the dishes is countless. The number of bacteria clinging to and floating in the dishes is also unimaginable. Those at the same table, carelessly unaware, use the same cups and chopsticks and eat the leftovers, they are swallowing tuberculosis bacteria.

IV.

Alas, if someone suffering from tuberculosis is a guest, they may be able to avoid infection during one or two shared meals. But for family members, fathers and sons, living and working together, seeing each other every day, sharing every meal, eating together two or three times a day, they are taking tuberculosis bacteria into their bodies. How can they avoid infection? Therefore, I say that to offend this danger is no different from stepping on a sword's edge or walking through fire. Those who are not infected may have special physical conditions that allow them to escape. But how can we rely on this? Although tuberculosis is mostly transmitted through the air, the food we eat is also a path to disaster. Then, the practice of shared meals is a system of taking tuberculosis bacteria daily to satiate the healthy. Isn't this a bad habit? Shouldn't those who know their fate be afraid and wary? Shouldn't virtuous people loudly condemn and eliminate it? The number of tuberculosis patients in China is truly staggering. Like a vast flood, we do not know where the inundation will end. This is also the source of national weakness and racial decline. Those who care about the world should pay attention to this point of custom reform. (This article is reprinted from Mr. Yu's Medical Discourse)

A Lung Specimen Prepared by Dr. Dender of Germany

The Latest Treatment for Tuberculosis

The cause of pulmonary tuberculosis (i.e., tuberculosis) is the tubercle bacillus. Once this bacterium enters the human body, it forms a nodule at that location, cutting off the blood supply. Furthermore, the tubercle bacillus secretes an acid-resistant waxy substance that surrounds its body to protect itself from the intrusion of all external medicinal forces. Therefore, although various bactericidal drugs are taken internally or injected, they cannot reach the substance of the germ itself. The natural therapy, symptomatic therapy, physical therapy, serum therapy, drug therapy, and all other therapies that doctors have traditionally used have not been completely successful, and the saying that there is no cure for lung disease has spread throughout the world because this profound theory is unknown. Based on the above theory, modern tuberculosis scholars continue to research tirelessly, and as a result, they have achieved this chemical saint agent that kills all tuberculosis bacteria, named Sanosin. This drug was successfully invented based on the latest medical theories of Dr. Koch of Germany, the inventor of the tubercle bacillus, and Dr. Berger of Germany, the inventor of the tubercle bacillus dewaxing technique. According to the current experimental reports of various lung disease sanatoriums in Germany, Switzerland, and other countries, this drug has the effect of penetrating the nodules of lung lesions and dissolving the waxy substance. It also has bactericidal power and can fundamentally cure stage 1, 2, and 3 tuberculosis, with a guaranteed effect in every case. In China, the Pharmaceutical Testing Institute of the National Government has tested it and found that the medicine is mild, non-toxic, and has absolutely no side effects. Now, a brief description of its medicinal effect is given below:

(1) When the medicinal effect of "Sanosin" is experimentally tested in a test tube, the acid resistance of all tubercle bacilli disappears after one minute, and after three minutes, the tubercle bacilli are completely killed, with none spared.

(2) According to animal experiments, it was found that "Sanosin" can penetrate into tuberculous lesions. When examining the tubercle bacilli latent within the lesions, they were found to have completely lost their acid resistance. This proves that the waxy substance has been completely dissolved.

(3) If a patient takes "Sanosin" internally for about a week, they will immediately see good conditions such as sputum thinning and body heat decreasing.

(4) If "Sanosin" is continued internally for more than 30 to 60 days, a visible increase in body weight, increased appetite, and gradual relief of all symptoms will be apparent, ultimately achieving the great effect of bringing back the dead.

Report on the Experiment of "Three That Stars" and Guidance Book on Lung Disease Treatment Available Upon Request 68

American Trading Company, A. S. Watson & Company, Scientific Department, No. 35 Renji Road, Shanghai (at the intersection of Renji Road and Sichuan Road)

Summary of Important News

Chairman Ding Weifen presided over the meeting, and after the ceremony, He Yingqin gave a speech. He stated that today is the anniversary of May Ninth, which is the national humiliation day when Japanese imperialists presented the Twenty-One Demands in the fourth year of the Republic of China, coercing Yuan Shikai to sign. Yuan Shikai, in his plot to establish an empire, sacrificed national territory and sovereignty and succumbed to Japanese imperialists. However, the people fought hard and refused to recognize it, and the Japanese imperialists ultimately failed to obtain these rights. But Japanese imperialists never forget aggression, such as the Shanghai Massacre in the fourteenth year of the Republic of China, the Shaqi Massacre in Guangdong, and the Jinan Massacre in the seventeenth year of the Republic of China, all stemmed from aggressive intentions. Our people are deeply pained and will never forget this national humiliation. The most severe point of the Twenty-One Demands proposed by Japanese imperialists was to hand over our country's land and sovereignty to them. The significance of our meeting today is to remind all compatriots to remember clearly the various aggressive acts of Japanese imperialists against us, and to strive at all times to protect the interests and dignity of our people and the survival and prosperity of our nation. We must absolutely seek national independence and strength. When Japanese imperialists proposed these Twenty-One Demands, there were many traitors who acted as pawns for Japanese imperialists and Yuan Shikai. Yuan Shikai wanted to use the Twenty-One Demands as a condition for Japanese imperialists to first recognize his imperial system, so he did not hesitate to betray the country. Many unequal treaties were formed by traitorous officials and warlords who only sought personal gain and disregarded the great harm to the country. Sixteen years have passed since the national humiliation of May Ninth. Has the national humiliation been redressed? I am afraid that comrades will not be able to give a good answer. Various national humiliations are increasing day by day. On one hand, white imperialists are heavily oppressing us, and on the other hand, red imperialists are doing their best to attack us. Even in this campaign to suppress the Red bandits in the three provinces of Hunan, Hubei, and Jiangxi, many documents and slogans seized from the Red bandits show that red imperialists are behind them. Remote counties in the three provinces are plagued by Red bandits, and almost all houses are empty. The Red bandits' acts of betraying the country are so painful to the people, and this national humiliation must also be urgently redressed. Since the successful completion of the Northern Expedition and unification, some achievements have been made in diplomacy, such as the recovery of customs tariffs, the recovery of concessions, and the recovery of legal rights. It can be seen that resisting foreign aggression requires self-strengthening. Today, commemorating the national humiliation requires the people to sacrifice personal emotions and selfishness, and it requires the people to arouse national spirit and patriotic public-mindedness to serve the country together. Only then can the national humiliation be redressed, and the commemoration will have meaning. Our party's ideology and the instructions of the Premier are that we must realize the National Assembly and abolish unequal treaties in the shortest possible time. Now the National Assembly has been realized, and the abolition of unequal treaties must also be fully accomplished this year. I hope that comrades will strive for these last five minutes and work together to promote its realization. After the report, the ceremony was completed, and the meeting adjourned.

Tragedy at Hankou No. 42 Elementary School 70

Classroom Collapse Kills Two, Injures Dozens

Hankou Dispatch: At 10:00 AM on the 8th, a classroom in the second branch of the Hankou Municipal No. 42 Elementary School suddenly collapsed, killing two students, seriously injuring one, and leaving five missing. Dozens were slightly injured. This is an unprecedented tragedy in Hankou's educational circles. The school is located in the Model District. The first branch is in Yuyin Lane, and the second branch is in Yixiang Lane. It was originally the First Workers' School and was expanded in the 18th year of the Republic of China. The school building of the first branch is still solid, but the second branch had been occupied by troops for a long time, and frequent test firing of guns and bullets caused much damage to the walls. Due to limited funding, repairs could not be made. At 9:30 AM on the 8th, students from the second-year upper and second-year lower grades were combined in the upstairs classroom, and female teacher Xu Duanfang was teaching a music lesson when the entire building suddenly collapsed. Except for three or five students who managed to escape by grabbing onto doors and windows, the remaining 97 students and female teacher Xu Duanfang all fell together. Neighbors and the 48th Division Military Police Battalion rushed to rescue them, and many students were rescued from the rubble. Two students died immediately: Zhou Guangshi, 11 years old, and Wei Tianzhang, 10 years old. One student was seriously injured: Hu Huanyan, 10 years old. More than a dozen students were slightly injured, including Tian Jinye, Wang Youjin, Cao Hancheng, Qiu Liwen, Zhang Dezhong, Ye Wangbao, Weng Youyue, Li Youjun, Ding Xudong, Ren Ziru, Liu Ruoting, and Liang Bingjun. Female teacher Xu Duanfang was also slightly injured. Five others are missing, and it is not yet known whether they escaped and returned home or were buried in the rubble. After receiving the news, the Municipal Education Bureau immediately dispatched Han Lianhe, Chen Cairu, Liao Hong, and Zhao Liancheng to the scene to direct the rescue. The Municipal Government also sent Liu Jizhi to inspect and ordered the Municipal Hospital to send doctors Chen Binghua and Liu Shanqing to provide emergency treatment. The Security Team was ordered to rush to the scene to maintain order. The injured students and teachers were sent to the Municipal Hospital and the Catholic Church Hospital for treatment. Rao Chonggong, the school's director of moral education, went to the students' homes to offer condolences. Acting Mayor He Fuzhou of the Municipal Government telegraphed Mayor Liu Wendao about the incident, stating: "This afternoon, at the Yixiang Lane No. 42 Elementary School, while a music lesson was being taught upstairs, the building collapsed due to decay, killing two students, Wei Tianzhang and Zhou Guangshi, seriously injuring Hu Huanyan, and slightly injuring more than a dozen others. Upon receiving the report, workers and the Security Team and doctors were dispatched with medicine to provide assistance. The injured students have been sent to the Municipal Hospital for treatment. Arrangements are being made for the deceased students. The bureau has sent personnel to join school staff and doctors to provide condolences. Further reports will follow." The Municipal Education Bureau also convened an emergency meeting and resolved: (1) The school is ordered to promptly investigate and report the details of the casualties. (2) Request the Municipal Government to provide compensation for the deceased students. (3) Request the Municipal Hospital to provide free medical treatment for the injured students. (4) School Principal Zhou Fo is suspended from his duties, and Inspector Xiong Hongzhao is appointed to investigate and report. (5) Section staff Liao Hong will temporarily take charge of maintaining school affairs. (May 8th)

Bandits in Southern Shandong Being Suppressed 71

Ma Brigade Captures Dozens of Bandits Alive

Gu Division Orders Strict Suppression by All Units

Important Bandit Leaders Are Being Apprehended One After Another

Jinan Dispatch: After being routed by various army units, the remaining bandits in southern Shandong will be eliminated soon. The Jiang telegram from the Third Route Staff Office of the Teng County Anti-Bandit Command is recorded below: (1) According to the report from Brigade Commander Ma Dongwei, (A) The bandits in Huluo'ao are being suppressed by Dong Chenzhi's three regiments and the 13th Cavalry Company along the Jiquan-Liuquan line. The bandits stubbornly resisted, but after our fierce attack, they fled to Juliang Mountain and continued to resist from the stronghold. The 13th Company was ordered to launch several fierce attacks, but due to the dangerous terrain, they could not be eliminated. All three infantry regiments were then ordered to encircle Juliang Mountain, coordinating with Guo Regiment of Chen Division stationed in Gaozhuang, demarcating the northeast, south, and southwest sides of Juliang Mountain as our defensive lines. The western and southwestern mountain gullies would be Guo Regiment's defensive lines. The bandits, seeing the situation was critical, suddenly fled towards Huluo'ao from the southwestern mountain gully. The 13th Cavalry Company was ordered to pursue them. Due to the late hour, it was not convenient to pursue them relentlessly. It is estimated that about two to three hundred bandits fled this time, and many were killed by our machine guns or fell to their deaths in the mountain streams. (B) The remaining bandits here are scattered in small groups. The Third Infantry Regiment, attached with the Third Company of the Cavalry Battalion, has been ordered to search and attack along the Liuquan-Ji line towards Huluo'ao. According to Brigade Commander Ma Dongwei's telegram, (A) At 9:00 PM, the bandits on Juliang Mountain were severely attacked by Guo Regiment of Chen Division. A portion fled northwest and dozens were captured alive. One platoon leader and four soldiers from our unit were injured, and one platoon leader was killed. (B) The Third Infantry Regiment, attached with the Second Cavalry Company, has been ordered to strictly suppress the fleeing bandits and search for hidden bandits near Juliang Mountain. The Third Infantry Regiment, attached with the Second Cavalry Company, is pursuing them. (C) According to the captured bandits, the bandit leaders are mostly hiding, and scattered bandits are wearing military uniforms, secretly hiding weapons, and acting as scouts for the army. (2) According to the telegram from Division Commander Chen Dongwei, (A) The bandits occupying Juliang Mountain, Laotou Mountain, and Laoma Mountain were encircled by Dong Yixie and Ma Brigade on all sides. At 6:00 PM, they charged twice towards the defensive line of Xu Regiment to the west, but were repulsed by our army. They then broke out to the northwest and were ambushed by Chen Battalion at Laoshan Waist, suffering heavy casualties, with more than 30 bandits killed, two bandit family members captured, seven horses, more than ten mules, and six guns seized. The bandits then fled towards Jiaoshan area. (B) There are no more bandits at Juliang Mountain, Laotou Mountain, etc. A portion of Xu Regiment has been transferred to Juliang Mountain, while Guo Regiment is still searching for hidden bandits in Xiangshan, etc. (3) According to the telegram from Division Commander Gu Jiangwu, (A) The bandits attacking Huiquan Gu Mountain were surrounded by Li Battalion of Kong Regiment, and many bandits were killed by artillery fire. The remaining bandits fled southwest. (B) Tang Brigade and Kang Regiment are strictly searching along the mountain streams, while Xue Regiment is strictly searching the streams in the east and west Yangjiaquan areas. (C) About three hundred bandits occupying Da Xiaocang Mountain were ordered to be suppressed by the Engineer Battalion. According to reports, before reaching Cang Mountain, the bandits seized the opportunity to flee far north. (4) All units have been ordered to search and suppress the bandits in order to eliminate them as soon as possible. Seal of Jiangyou, Staff Office of the Third Route of Teng County.

Furthermore, a letter from Teng County reported on the bandit suppression situation, stating that many bandits have fled after being suppressed. Some are in groups of six or seven, others in groups of a dozen or more. The village militias have been exerting extraordinary efforts, searching everywhere, and blocking roads even at night. Each township captures and sends more than a dozen or twenty bandits to the city every day. A few days ago, it was discovered in Fanchuan District that bandit leader Wang Shiyuan (a major bandit leader for more than ten years) was hiding in a certain village. When attacking, the Qingxiang Brigade from the city also assisted. After fighting for a day, his house was burned down, and Wang Shiyuan and four of his accomplices were burned to death. His wife and four accomplices were captured alive. His wife identified them correctly, and their heads were cut off and photographed for reporting. In Menglitian District, giant bandit Cheng Liu, a native of Yi County, was captured yesterday, along with 1,200 silver dollars and considerable gold items. The merchant militia captured bandit leader Yu Hongxiang and five accomplices in Zhaogou Village. In addition to these three bandit leaders, many other less known bandits have been captured. Many captured Mauser pistols and rifles have been turned over to the respective districts for their own use. Therefore, the people all have the intention of getting rich and obtaining guns. Whenever they encounter bandits, they bravely capture them. (6th)

Xun Chamber of Commerce Petitions for the Abolition of the Jiujiang Regular Customs 72

Nanchang Correspondence: The Jiujiang General Chamber of Commerce held a joint meeting yesterday in Nanchang, resolving to petition the Ministry of Finance to, in accordance with the Central Government's resolution, promptly abolish the Jiujiang Regular Customs to comply with government orders and alleviate merchants' hardships. The original petition stated: "On April 2nd of this year, we received the Ministry's Guan Zi No. 1227 instruction, stating that the petitioner, Wang Rufang, Chairman of the Jiujiang General Chamber of Commerce, et al., submitted a document, approving the Hubei Inland Qiyang Timber Merchants Association's letter stating that small rafts transported from Han were sealed after passing through Jiujiang. They requested a detailed explanation of the true situation of the customs. The reply indicated that the case had already been instructed to the Timber Merchants Association for compliance, etc. We humbly note that within the resolution on abolishing likin in five provinces, the seventh item of the second step for abolishing regular customs stipulated that regular customs duties and surtaxes within fifty li of commercial ports should be completely abolished by the end of that year (the 19th year [of the Republic, i.e., 1930]). This grand resolution has spread far and wide, and all Chinese people who heard it were delighted. However, Hubei had already abolished them, while Jiujiang still retains them. What one has, the other lacks. Taxation is unequal, which is of no benefit to the country but only harms the people. The government's prestige and the people's sentiments are greatly affected, so we must report this to the Ministry. The Jiujiang Regular Customs has been established for a long time. Now, the new customs tariff, new business tax regulations, and five consolidated taxes have all been implemented in order. If all revenues can be collected for public use, the national treasury's income will be ample. If the regular customs duties are not resolutely abolished, it will not affect other tax revenues in the end. The Ministry spares no effort in reorganizing finances and eliminates evil completely. How can it retain this corrupt practice and discriminate against the Jiangxi people, causing the world to criticize it? This is the first reason why respecting the government's prestige requires the abolition of the Jiujiang Regular Customs. Our party's revolution was originally to relieve the suffering of the people and eliminate excessive levies. Since the Ministry convened a five-province conference on abolishing likin and resolved to abolish all regular customs within fifty li of commercial ports in phases, except for the three regular customs on the land borders, the Jiujiang Regular Customs still exists. Everyone else benefits, but we alone are left out. Moreover, the disparity in taxation concerns the rise and fall of commerce. Merchants, due to the heavy taxes in Jiujiang, have changed their routes to other places, causing Jiujiang's commerce to decline and Hubei's commerce to develop. Is Hubei moving towards the Three Principles of the People, while Jiangxi is independent in a different realm? What is the meaning of national equality and a world for all? Our government treats the people like wounded, and should treat everyone equally, and should not do this. Moreover, in recent years, banditry has been rampant, wealth has been exhausted, and the people are impoverished, with almost no survivors. As the ancient saying goes, wealth gathers when the people scatter, and wealth scatters when the people gather. Extending a lifeline to the people of Jiangxi is to cultivate a portion of vitality for the country. This is the second reason why considering the people's sentiments requires the abolition of the Jiujiang Regular Customs. The affiliated association leads the merchants and dares to express their feelings and plead. We implore the Ministry to carefully examine and consider the merchants' hardships and swiftly resolve this matter to comfort the people's expectations. We are extremely anxious and await your orders." (May 8th)

Strike at Lieshan Coal Mine in Sixian County 73

Due to Complications Arising from the Arrest of Bandits by Garrison Troops

Bengbu Correspondence: The Lieshan Coal Mine in Sixian County is the most famous mineral production in Anhui Province. The annual output of coal exceeds ten million tons, and the fuel for the three provinces of Jiangsu, Anhui, and Henan mostly relies on it. Since the autumn of last year, the Lieshan Coal Mine Bureau was reorganized into the state-private joint Lieshan Coal Mine Company. The board of directors actively repaired the damaged coal mines in the mining area. Currently, there are three intact coal mines that can produce 300 tons of coal per day. In October last year, the Anhui Garrison Second Brigade, under Chen Xiaosi, was transferred from western Shandong to Anhui. The mining authorities then requested and obtained Chairman Chen's approval to have the Song Battalion of the Qu Zheng Regiment of the Chen Brigade stationed at Lieshan to protect the coal mine. Before long, the Chen Brigade was transferred to western Anhui to suppress the communists, and the company's original mine police were responsible for protection. In March of this year, Wang Jun, the commander of the Jinpu Railway Garrison, deployed troops to garrison the Sixian County area along the Jinpu Line, taking charge of protecting the railway. All areas within fifty li on both sides of the railway belonged to the garrison area. The Lieshan Coal Mine Company, because the area around the mine was entirely bandit territory and the bandits were exceptionally rampant, and because the mining area was located within fifty li west of the railway (Lieshan is only forty-five li from Fuliji), petitioned Wang Jun to send troops to be stationed at Lieshan for protection. Wang, because his troops needed to concentrate on training, initially did not immediately approve. Last month, Wang ordered the Gong Chaomei Regiment of the Twentieth Brigade stationed in Sixian to send the third battalion commander, Li Peng, to lead troops to search and suppress the bandits in the Caili area. On the second of this month, Li, based on a report, believed that there were bandits hiding near the Lieshan mining area. He then led eight soldiers from the Suixi battalion headquarters to Lieshan for inspection. As soon as they arrived at the street entrance, they saw a person standing by the side of the street eating zongzi, appearing suspicious. Just as they were about to go forward to inquire, the person hurriedly fled into a restaurant beside the street and opened fire. Li Peng's horse was immediately wounded. Li then ordered the soldiers to fire back. The Lieshan mine protection team, upon hearing the news, also came out to assist in the attack. For a time, the sound of gunfire was incessant. The soldiers and police also set fire to the restaurant's thatched house. The bandit then committed suicide inside. Li's unit captured a Mauser pistol. Afterwards, Li, believing that there were bandits in the mining area, thought that the mine workers were colluding with them. That night, he deployed two companies to Lieshan, thoroughly searching the coal factory and nearby houses, arresting several mine workers and taking them to the battalion headquarters for interrogation. In the following days, he arrested more than thirty workers. Yesterday (the 6th), he also arrested Xu Ziqin, the well work manager of the engineering department. As a result, the workers in each coal mine went on strike and fled one after another, causing the mining work to be suspended. Lu Zidong, the general manager of the Lieshan General Company, upon receiving the report, immediately went from Bengbu to Xuzhou to meet Wang Jun, requesting that he promptly stop Li's unit from arresting workers. Assistant Manager Wu Zijiu will also go to Beijing from Bengbu to report to the board of directors and submit a document to the Ministry of Industry to report the incident, so they can investigate and handle it. (May 7th)

The Loss and Aftermath of the Haiyuan Pavilion Collection (Continued) 74

At the time when the Yang family was transporting the books, the local government here had already received a report from Liaocheng, deeply fearing that they would flow into foreign lands. There was a time when considerable measures were taken. At the same time, newspapers everywhere reported it one after another. The provincial government and the Department of Education had successively received letters from both the Ministry of Interior and the Ministry of Education, inquiring about this case. The Department of Education and the Department of Civil Affairs then dispatched personnel to jointly investigate and properly devise a plan for the aftermath and safekeeping. I was one of the personnel dispatched by the Department of Education. The result of the joint investigation with the Department of Civil Affairs was roughly the same as the aforementioned. We also contacted the Yang residence and received their reply, stating that the remaining books stored in Liaocheng had indeed been transported here in their entirety and were currently nailed up in boxes. Because the grand lady was ill, they had no time to examine them. Once she recovered from her illness and the arrangement was complete, they would invite people from all walks of life to visit again. Since I had received a clear order to devise a proper safekeeping plan and had also received questions from people everywhere who were concerned about this matter, stating that the Yang family's collection of books was very important to culture and that the provincial library had a responsibility to devise a secure plan for it, the one who criticized the most strongly was Mr. Zheng Yuanju of Qingdao. Under this clear order and criticism, I first indirectly asked the Yang family for their opinion. As a result, the Yang family also very much wanted a proper safekeeping plan. They instructed me to first state the library's opinions and outline them for their consideration. After consulting with the supervising officer and obtaining his agreement, I put forward three plans as a draft. In the late part of this month, I entrusted someone to deliver it to the Yang family. Up to now, I have not received a formal reply. I only received a letter from Mr. Yang Jingfu, saying, "I have just received your letter. I have learned everything with respect. I am always grateful for your concern. As for the draft agreement, I will reply in detail in another letter. I am writing to inform you first." Apart from this, there was also an indirect verbal expression that after the grand lady recovered from her illness, she would invite important relatives and family members to discuss it in detail before replying. This matter concerns the Yang family themselves and all aspects, so it cannot be handled carelessly. Before receiving a reply, the news I received from the Yang family was that the grand lady and trusted family members, in view of the changes in the world in recent years, had a tendency to comply with the library's proposals. They had no preconceived notions about these three plans and were planning to make an unprecedented righteous act in the cultural aspect of the entire province in order to honor their ancestors. However, they must wait until Mr. Yang Jingfu comes to Jinan before they can make a final decision. The quarterly journal is about to be published. What I should report to the country about this case is also up to the present situation. How to reply in the future and all the aftermath will not be allowed by the time at this moment. However, I will attach the proposal made by our library to the Yang family (the terms, namely the draft outline of the agreement, have been recorded in the previous report) for the reference of those who are concerned about this matter. At the same time, regarding the Yang family's collection of books, I dare to make the following conclusion based on my personal observations: The Yang family's first transfer of rare books to Tianjin was in view of the local chaos during the Zhang Zongchang era, when his subordinates often thought of seizing them for themselves. For the sake of preservation and safety, they had no choice but to handle it in this way. It was not to sell them in Tianjin. The second transfer to Jinan was also really forced by the bandit turmoil in recent years. There was no other intention. Judging from the facts and speaking fairly, both transfers of books were very proper actions. With millions of heavy items, who would deliberately move them unless it was absolutely necessary? The one to blame for being forced to do this should be the environment, not the Yang family. If there had been no first transfer of books, then in this turmoil, the seeds of Tao Nan's rare books would have been cut off from then on. As far as I know, Yang Jingfu is indeed very upright and honest. As for his grand lady, she is painstakingly guarding the books, betting her life on them. We especially admire her decisive spirit. However, today's situation is not what it used to be. What we hope for from the Yang family is to repeatedly change their previous rigid viewpoint and make arrangements that are beneficial to themselves and others for permanent preservation. At the same time, social people, if they really love books and love culture, should also put themselves in the Yang family's shoes and devise a way out for them, and should not make irresponsible criticisms and empty talk, or force the parties to dispel their original intention of sharing their goodness with others in the heat of passion. Everyone can know the preciousness of the Yang family's books. Everyone can say that they are related to culture and should be preserved and not lost. However, the degree of their knowledge may stop there. If you ask them how to find a way and how to preserve them, they will stare blankly and be unable to answer. Furthermore, if you ask them to find a way and handle it, they will be even more hesitant and avoid it, not daring to admit it themselves and not wanting to be involved in the slightest, while the laughter and scolding behind their backs remain the same. Alas, is this what those who love people with virtue should do? (The End)

Local Correspondence

Songjiang 75

The First Battalion of the Security Force Escorts the Arrested Bandits

Bai, the commander of the first battalion of the second regiment of the security force, continued to lead the team to suppress bandits in the southern countryside and search for bandits. Now, they have arrested the key bandit Song Aqiu, who confessed to robbing the Yuan Shutang family with Pan Amu. Yu Alai confessed to robbing and extorting with Song Fushou in various cases. Ping Ada, Zhang Amei, Shi Agen, Zhu Dagen, etc. were also apprehended and escorted to the headquarters for interrogation. It is reported that Ping is suspected of contacting bandits to redeem tickets. Zhang confessed to robbing the Ma Shenfang, Du Xiaoqing, and Wu Awu families in Queyu Fang. Zhu Dagen also confessed to robbing the Li Ajin family in Nanlu and the He Chunrong families in Qiu Fu Temple with Wang Azhao. Shi Agen confessed to being dragged by Tao Ada to row boats, etc. They have already been interrogated and detained pending verification.

Nanhui 76

The Entire County Party Committee Dismissed Due to a Case

Chen Shixian, Pan Yu, and Shi Shunyuan, members of the county party reorganization committee, have been dismissed from all their positions due to the occurrence of a serious case. The provincial party reorganization committee has resolved this, and dispatched personnel to take custody beforehand. Yesterday, the custodian Zhu arrived in Nanhui to take over.

Tax Collection Official Absconds Due to Owed Taxes

Gu Xinchen, a tax collection official from the Nineteenth Bao and Twenty-eighth Tu of the Sixth District, has accumulated tax arrears over the years, amounting to approximately 1,700 yuan. Unable to repay, he suddenly absconded yesterday. Gu Changfu and others, members of the said Tu, reported this to the Sixth District Office, requesting that a letter be forwarded to the county finance bureau, ordering the environmental protection person, Min Yushan, to pay the compensation to recover public funds.

Suzhou 77

Strict Investigation of Rice Smuggling

Huang, the county magistrate of Wu County, upon learning that local rice prices have recently soared and the people are shaken, and hearing rumors that unscrupulous merchants, disregarding the overall situation, are smuggling and selling rice overseas for profit, which violates the principles of food management, specifically issued an order yesterday (the 9th) to the district chiefs of each district to conduct a strict investigation. If there is any smuggling overseas, it should be quickly investigated and reported for legal action.

Reappointment of Wardens of Three County Detention Centers

On the 9th, the High Court announced that Jin Hao, warden of the Jiangning District Court Detention Center, had resigned with approval. His vacancy was filled by Gong Kuan from Jiangdu. The vacancy left by Gong Kuan in Jiangdu was filled by Han Minwen from Zhenjiang. The vacancy in Zhenjiang was temporarily filled by Zhang Ruiqiang, section chief of the No. 2 section of the Third Prison, appointed by the ministry. Before Han's vacancy arrives, it will be temporarily held by Peng Yicheng.

Wuxi 78

Large Quantities of Military Firepower and Opium Seized

The officers and soldiers of the Eighth Company of the Fourth Regiment of the Xichang Gendarmerie seized two boxes of Mauser pistols, each box containing forty-seven pieces, and ten boxes of bullets, totaling 50,000 rounds, at the railway station the night before last. Since there was no one to claim them and no formal passport, they were detained together and reported to Company Commander Hu, who sent several soldiers to escort the military firepower to the regimental headquarters for investigation and handling. Also, the battalion headquarters of the Second Battalion of the said regiment, while inspecting passengers on the Jinghu train the night before last, seized a large quantity of opium, weighing approximately 400 kilograms, divided into eight sacks (worth more than 10,000 yuan). At the same time, they also arrested a red pill peddler, Pan Mingde, and found ten small packets of red pills (a total of 100,000 pills). They were immediately taken to the battalion headquarters and transferred to the regimental headquarters. Yesterday, acting regimental commander Ying prepared a document and sent a team to escort them to the Capital Garrison Headquarters for punishment.

Changzhou 79

Gendarmes Arrest a Fake Military Officer

Sui Zongxi, acting commander of the Third Regiment of the Changzhou Gendarmerie, the night before last sent his subordinate Zhang Baozhi along with soldiers to inspect various hotels. When inspecting room number two of the Shengping Hotel on County Zhijie Street, a guest named Guo Jun (styled Tianmin) appeared flustered and was immediately searched. A name card of a counselor of the General Headquarters of the Army, Navy, and Air Force was found. Under questioning, it was found that he was an imposter and falsely claimed to be a graduate of the first class of the Whampoa Military Academy. He was immediately taken to the regimental headquarters for interrogation.

The Truth of the Suspected Death Case Gradually Becomes Clear

In the suspected corpse case found in the Sixth District of Wuyi, it is now known that the deceased's name is Wu Lianfa, a native of Yutang Village near Qishuyan. He worked as a tea servant at the Shanghai Oriental Hotel. He had a hidden illness. Recently, he returned home to collect debts. While passing through Huangjiatan, villagers, suspecting his actions, beat him and sent him to Luoyang Town. Then he was carried back to Huangjiatan and died from his injuries. The deceased's family learned the details and are now negotiating.

Nantong 80

Zhang Jian's Property Awaits Provincial Orders for Return

Zhang Jian, a native of the county, was wanted and his property was seized in the 16th year of the Republic (1927) for colluding with the enemy. The provincial government has now received an order from Chairman Chiang to revoke Zhang Jian's punishment in accordance with the New Year's Day amnesty. The provincial government's Department of Civil Affairs has telegraphed the Nantong County government to temporarily postpone the disposal of Zhang's property. How to return it awaits further orders.

Preventing and Suppressing Bandits in the Eastern Countryside

Recently, bandits have been harassing various districts in the eastern countryside of Tongyi. The county government has sent police teams to defend and suppress them, and has also transferred pacification troops and the Tonghaiqi guerrilla forces to assist in the suppression. County Magistrate Zhang went to various districts in person on the 8th to inspect the situation.

Ningbo 81

The Kidnapped Sun Surname Ticket Was Rescued from Danger

The eldest and second grandsons of Sun Zhishou, a wealthy gentry of Sun Lane in Yuyao, were kidnapped at the same time last month and a huge ransom was demanded. It is now learned that the Yuyao-based Third Battalion Headquarters, based on a tip-off the night before last, said that the Sun surname ticket was hidden in the Shuiyinpu area. They immediately led soldiers there, smashed the bandit's den, captured three bandits, and rescued two tickets. They have now been sent to the county's rural cleansing bureau for investigation and handling.

Mingguang 82

Spring Rains Cause Disaster

Recently, continuous torrential rains have lasted for more than ten days. In the past two days, there have been thunderstorms, with the intensity of a downpour, lasting for two days and nights. As a result, mountain floods broke out and rivers overflowed. The fields along the river have all become swamps. It is estimated that more than 100 hectares of wheat fields in Hongmiao, Jiaocheng, Chendui, Qili, Jianxi, and other lakes have been submerged. Dozens of houses have collapsed in the main roads and west of the river, but fortunately, no one was injured.

This City's Various Circles Do Not Forget the "May 9th" National Humiliation 83

Yesterday, a Memorial Meeting Was Held at the City Party Headquarters

Advocating Resisting Japanese Goods to Avenge This Singular Disgrace

Yesterday (the 9th) was the 16th anniversary of the "May 9th" National Humiliation. The Shanghai Special City Party Headquarters Propaganda Department specially convened people from all walks of life to hold a memorial meeting in the auditorium on the third floor of the City Party Headquarters. More than 800 representatives from various circles attended. The meeting was presided over by Yang Qingyuan, Minister of the City Propaganda Department, who reported the facts of the "May 9th" National Humiliation and gave detailed instructions on how to avenge the humiliation. Afterwards, the representatives successively gave speeches and shouted slogans before the meeting adjourned.

City Party Headquarters

Meeting Order (1) Stand at attention in unison; (2) Sing the Party song; (3) Pay the highest respects to the Party and National flags and the portrait of the late Premier; (4) Chairman respectfully reads the late Premier's will; (5) Observe silence; (6) Chairman's report; (7) Speeches; (8) Shout slogans; (9) Adjournment.

Attending Representatives Representatives from the Social Affairs Bureau, the Discussion Committee of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, the Municipal Government, the Shanghai Office of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, the Municipal Chamber of Commerce, the First District Party Headquarters, the Second District Party Headquarters, the Third District Party Headquarters, the Fourth District Party Headquarters, the Fifth District Party Headquarters, the Li Jiao Federation, the Citizens' Association, the Pharmaceutical Workers' Union, the Shipbuilding Workers' Union, the Hat-Making Workers' Union, the Toothbrush Industry Workers' Union, the Boy Scout Council, the Cigarette Workers' Union, the Silk Reeling Workers' Union, the Publishing Workers' Union, the Cosmetics Trade Association, and other labor groups, as well as representatives from various schools and Party headquarters at all levels, totaling more than 800 people.

Chairman's Report Comrades, representatives, today is the anniversary of the "May 9th" National Humiliation. Our people are intellectually immature, politically corrupt, culturally backward, and industrially declining. Moreover, our country is vast in territory and rich in resources, but production is not yet wealthy, so it is suitable to be the target of imperialist aggression, the fish and meat on the chopping board. Before the Meiji Restoration in Japan, the weakness of its national power and the shackles of unequal treaties were no less difficult than in our country. However, after the Restoration, the whole country, from top to bottom, united to work hard and govern diligently. In a few years, unequal treaties were lifted, international status was restored, and industry developed and thrived, and the national power was rising day by day. However, the territory is small and the raw materials are lacking, especially the two important raw materials for industrial development, coal and iron. The domestic population is also increasing day by day. Therefore, in order to complete the solid foundation of imperialism, it turned from an oppressed nation into an oppressing nation. However, all the weak nations in the world are slaughtered by the world powers, and the development in the east, west, south, and north is hindered. Therefore, they went west to attack our vast Republic of China, which is vast in territory and rich in resources. At first, in the Sino-Japanese War, our navy was defeated, and we ceded land and paid reparations, and the losses were great. Later, Japan believed that Russia was also invading our country in the same way, and the interests conflicted, so it decided to fight. After the Russo-Japanese War, Russia was defeated miserably, so Japan was complacent, looked down on the world, and was booming and hot. Then, the European War broke out, and the European and American powers were busy fighting each other and had no time to look east. Japan thought that this opportunity was hard to come by. At that time, it was precisely the time to invade our great Republic of China with great fanfare, an opportunity that would not come for thousands of years. Therefore, under the pretext of declaring war on Germany, it seized our Qingdao and occupied the Jiaoji Railway, and put forward twenty-one articles. The insane and mad pseudo-government of Beijing, under the guise of loan relations, actually recognized it. However, our people unanimously opposed it, and without legal signature recognition, the treaty was invalid. However, after a careful examination of the twenty-one articles, we can see a glimpse of the Japanese people's intentions. Now, it may be useful to briefly analyze it. The content of the first item is to seize the rights to port bays, railways, and mines leased by Germany in Shandong Province. The second item is to actively annex our Manchuria and Mongolia. The third item is to seize the right to dispose of the assets of the Hanyeping Company and the right to exploit nearby mines. The fourth item is to encompass all the ports and islands along our coast. The fifth item is to monopolize our domestic affairs, such as military police, finance, transportation, and culture. From this, it can be seen that the Japanese want to destroy our country and exterminate our species. Since the fourth year of the Republic of China, the Japanese policy of invading our country has been consistent from beginning to end. The May 30th Massacre in Shanghai and the May 3rd Jinan Massacre after the Northern Expeditionary Army rose up have emerged one after another, and they all want to destroy our country before they are happy. Recently, our country has been working hard to govern and is seeking construction. The status of the National Government is becoming more and more consolidated. In addition to jealousy, the Japanese people have taken advantage of some misunderstandings in the two Guangdong provinces to fabricate rumors and sow discord, lest our country be in chaos. All our people should be alarmed by the sinister intentions and poisonous methods. Today, we solemnly commemorate the "May 9th" National Humiliation. If we want to avenge the humiliation and wash away the shame, we can only do so if the whole country, from top to bottom, is of one heart and one mind. The only shortcut is to resist Japanese goods. Our country's resistance to Japanese goods did not start today, but unfortunately, we have repeatedly spoken of resistance, but we have repeatedly lacked perseverance, which has led to the failure to achieve the effect of resistance, but has instead left foreigners with the ridicule of a five-minute fever. After shame and anger, we should strengthen our will and unify our steps, and take the resistance to foreign goods as an important task of our people. Then, Japan, which sells 54% of its products to our country every year, will inevitably face economic panic and collapse. Since the increase in customs tariffs, in the recent two or three months, Japanese people have established more than 500 factories in various parts of Shanghai. Their sinister intentions are like this. Can our people not be careful? This is the first point that we should strive for in commemorating the "May 9th" National Humiliation. Second, eliminate the Red bandits. The Red bandits are a disaster to our country's interior and are a serious problem. If this is not eliminated, not only will the internal strife continue, but also the industry will never have the hope of revival. The livelihood problem and the revolutionary construction will all become empty talk. In the future, the government will continue to work hard to eliminate them step by step. The people should also devote themselves to the Baojia movement to defend themselves. Third, the National Assembly, which the whole country is looking forward to, held its first official meeting on the 8th, gathering elites from all over the country. Gathering together, discussing the major affairs of the Party and the country, we will be able to get to the point of the current situation, and the abolition of unequal treaties is the top priority of our country today. I think the National Assembly will pay attention to this and have practical measures, so that the success of diplomacy depends on whether the people have a strong backing. I hope that the compatriots in this city will devote themselves to national diplomacy in order to achieve the victory of the government's diplomacy. Today, on the occasion of the extremely painful commemoration of the "May 9th" National Humiliation, I put forward these three points as encouragement to the attending representatives and all the citizens. Afterwards, representatives such as Jin Xihan successively gave speeches, and the words were omitted due to length.

Meeting Slogans (1) Do not forget the May 9th National Humiliation; (2) Abolish consular jurisdiction; (3) Recover all concessions in the country; (4) Abolish all unequal treaties; (5) Overthrow Japanese imperialism; (6) Continue to resist foreign goods; (7) Support the National Assembly; (8) Strive for revolutionary construction; (9) Long live the Chinese Kuomintang; (10) Long live the Republic of China.

Announce Territorial Sea Boundary Line 84

Regulations on the Scope of Smuggling Suppression by Customs

Japanese fishing boats have repeatedly been heard to have invaded our country's territorial waters. In order to prevent such incidents from happening again, the central ministries have held meetings to clearly define and publicize the territorial sea boundary line. Since the territorial sea boundary line is stipulated, no fishing boats of any country are allowed to invade it in order to maintain sovereignty. The Ministry of Finance has also clearly stipulated the scope of smuggling suppression. It has now been decided to publicize it. Yesterday, the local shipping companies received an order from the Ministry forwarded by the Shipping Association, which said: The case is based on Instruction No. 1613 of the Ministry of Communications, and the case is based on an outline of the Instruction of the Executive Yuan: In the past, the Ministry of Interior, Foreign Affairs, Finance, Navy, and Industry jointly requested the planning of the territorial sea boundary line and the scope of smuggling suppression by customs in order to protect sovereignty. It has now been submitted to the 21st State Council meeting of this court for resolution. The scope of the territorial sea is set at three nautical miles, and the scope of smuggling suppression by customs is set at twelve nautical miles. The Ministry of Finance is to formulate the implementation and announcement measures for the scope of smuggling suppression and submit them for review. In addition to submitting them to the National Government for record and ordering the Ministry of Finance to comply with them, they are also ordered to be known and to inform their subordinates to be known in the same way (omitted below).

Eurasia Aviation Corporation Announces Postponement of Inaugural Flight 85

Rescheduled to May 31st

The Shanghai-Manzhouli air route planned by Eurasia Aviation Corporation was originally scheduled to officially open on the 15th of this month. The company officially notified this newspaper yesterday that it would change the date to May 31st to start postal transportation. The Shanghai-Manzhouli flight route is 10,000 kilometers long and can be reached in one and a half days, which is five or six days faster than ordinary postal delivery. In the future, beacons will be installed at each station to prepare for night flights, so that this route can be connected with the air routes of Soviet Russia and Germany, and the postal route from Shanghai to Europe can be reached in three days.

Reasons for Postponement Eurasia Aviation Corporation sent a letter to this newspaper yesterday, saying: In reply, the Shanghai-Manzhouli air route of our company was originally scheduled to officially open on May 15th to carry mail. The preparations have been completed. However, Chief Ke of the Postal Liaison Office of the Directorate General of Posts informed Li Jingzong, director of the company's operations department, on the 8th of this month that the issue of charging for air mail sent from abroad to China has not yet been sent to the International Postal Union. If the flight opens on the 15th, I am afraid that there will be no mail to transport from the plane returning from Manzhouli. In order to maintain the company's business interests, it is decided to officially open the flight on May 31st (Sunday). In addition to sending letters separately, this letter is sent for your reference.

Postal Transportation Schedule Eurasia Corporation has now decided to only carry mail and not passengers for the time being. The postal transportation schedule is as follows: (Shanghai to Manzhouli) Shanghai departure, every Wednesday and Sunday morning at 5:00, Nanjing arrival at 6:45 a.m., Nanjing departure at 7:30 a.m., Jinan arrival at 11:15 a.m., Jinan departure at 12:00 noon, Beijing arrival at 2:30 p.m., Beijing departure at 3:00 p.m., Duolun arrival at 6:30 p.m., Duolun departure every Thursday and Monday morning at 6:00, Manzhouli arrival at 12:00 noon, (Manzhouli to Shanghai) Manzhouli departure every Sunday and Tuesday morning at 9:00, Duolun arrival at 3:00 p.m., Duolun departure at 3:45 p.m., Beijing arrival at 7:15 p.m., Beijing departure every Monday and Wednesday morning at 4:00, Jinan arrival at 6:30 a.m., Jinan departure at 7:15 a.m., Nanjing arrival at 11:00 a.m., Nanjing departure at 11:45 a.m., Shanghai arrival at 1:30 p.m.

Representatives of the National Coal Production and Sales Association Petition in Beijing 87

Audience with Commanders-in-Chief Jiang and Deputy Commander Zhang

Requesting the Recovery of Kailuan and Other Three Items

And Submitting a Request to the Ministry of Railways to Reduce Freight Rates

According to the Nichinichi Shimbun, the National Coal Production and Sales Association has appointed Yu Shunqing, Zhang Zilian, and Huang Jicheng as representatives to go to Beijing today to petition Commander-in-Chief Jiang and Northeast Deputy Commander Zhang. At the same time, they will submit a request to the Ministry of Railways to reduce the freight rates for domestic coal. The text of the petition is recorded below:

Petition to Jiang and Zhang The case is to state three points, recommend representatives, and visit to petition. The Kailuan Company's joint venture agreement was signed in June of the first year of the Republic of China. Article 17 stipulates that ten years after the signing of this contract, the Luanzhou Company shall have the right to buy back all the assets of the Kaiping Company at a fair value agreed upon by both parties. To this day, the deadline has long passed. The Luanzhou Company has failed to prepare the price for the buyback, losing its sovereignty. The Kaiping Company relies on unequal treaties as a talisman to manipulate China's coal market, so that China's coal is squeezed out and cannot develop. It should be ordered that the Luanzhou Company prepare the price for the buyback. If the Luanzhou Company is unable to handle it or delays it, the government should raise funds to redeem it. This is the first thing to petition for. The stockpiles of coal in various mines are mountainous, but the roads do not allocate vehicles for transportation, resulting in coal shortages in various places. Various factories are in danger of suspending work. At this time, when domestic goods are sprouting, they are fighting fiercely with foreign goods. If they suspend work, they will give foreign goods an opportunity to take advantage of. It should be ordered that the Beining Railway Bureau allocate as many vehicles as possible to transport Datong, Jingxing,

Page 14

Liugegou, Tongbao, Zhengfeng, and the stockpiles of coal in various mines under Hebei Province to save the coal shortage. This is the second thing to petition for. There are various reasons why domestic coal cannot develop, and the fact that foreign coal relies on unequal treaties to enjoy the right to specially reduced freight rates is the main reason for restricting the development of our country's coal. Therefore, the association has proposed a proposal to reduce the freight rates for domestic coal in the National Business and Transportation Conference to provide relief. Today, domestic coal is becoming more and more declining, and the Jiaoji Railway Bureau suddenly increased the coal freight rates by 20% from May 1st. This is not only failing to reduce the rates, but also intensifying the situation. It should be ordered that the Jiaoji Railway Bureau cancel the new regulations and continue to charge according to the old regulations. In addition, all roads should follow the old regulations regarding coal freight rates. This is the third thing to petition for. In summary, the above three points are of great importance to the national economy and people's livelihood. It is appropriate to appoint Zhang Zilian, Huang Jicheng, and Yu Shunqing as representatives to hold a petition to visit your seat. I implore you to examine and approve it and issue orders separately to directly relieve domestic coal and indirectly promote domestic goods. It is a public convenience. Respectfully presented to Commander-in-Chief Jiang of the Army, Navy, and Air Force and Deputy Commander Zhang, Lin Kanghou, Chairman of the National Coal Production and Sales Association of the Republic of China, Standing Committee Members Fang Jiaobo, Hong Yanbin, Sheng Pihua, and Liu Yumen, respectfully presented.

Petition to the Ministry of Railways The case is for petitioning. The decline of domestic coal urgently needs to be relieved. The association has been running around and appealing, originally hoping to promote and develop it. It has submitted a proposal to the Business and Transportation Conference convened and convened by your ministry, requesting discussion of relief measures. At that time, it was resolved that the freight rates should be considered based on the coal production cost and selling price of each mine, etc. In addition, the Jiaoji Railway Administration sent a letter No. 963 Jiazi to the association on November 30 of last year, stating: After our road implemented the Ministry-issued tiered freight rates on November 1st, outsiders did not understand and thought that the freight rates had increased. There were many misunderstandings regarding coal. According to the new freight rates, coal is included in the sixth class. According to the old freight rates, the average reduction is 30%. The export coal price is still charged at 2.52 yuan per ton, and there has been no change so far. I am deeply afraid that the rumors will spread and the misunderstandings will become deeper. I hereby send this letter for your reference and to inform your colleagues so as to avoid misunderstandings, etc. Each is on file. Now I hear that the Jiaoji Railway Administration has decided to increase the coal freight rates by 20% from May 1st of this year. Coal merchants and merchants are terrified after listening. The domestic coal is being squeezed out by foreign coal and is struggling on the verge of death. Helping it and supporting it may have the hope of development. Now, suddenly, when domestic coal is beyond redemption, the freight rates are increased again. This is a plan to add insult to injury. The matter is of great importance to the national economy and people's livelihood. The association's heart is in danger and dares not remain silent. It is reasonable to present it to your ministry for examination and approval. I implore you to order the Jiaoji Railway Administration to cancel the previous proposal and continue to handle it according to the old regulations in order to maintain it and relieve the business difficulties. It is a public convenience. In addition to sending letters separately, respectfully presented to the Ministry of Railways, Lin Kanghou, Chairman of the National Coal Production and Sales Association of the Republic of China, Standing Committee Members Fang Jiaobo, Hong Yanbin, Sheng Pihua, and Liu Yumen, respectfully presented.

Two Legal Groups Sent Letters to the Tianjin Chamber of Commerce

Asking for Substantial Assistance

The National Chamber of Commerce Federation of the Republic of China and the National Federation of Industrial Associations sent a letter to the Tianjin Chamber of Commerce yesterday, saying: Domestic factories use Kailuan coal as the main fuel. In recent months, Kailuan coal has not arrived in port, and various factories have not purchased and stockpiled coal in advance due to economic reasons. Coal prices have soared for a while, with an average daily loss of about hundreds of thousands of yuan. Industrial stagnation and labor unemployment have been greatly affected, not only by Japanese coal taking the opportunity to seize the market. In addition to telegraphing the government for relief, we have also publicly appointed Dr. Qian Chengxu, director of the National Federation of Industrial Associations, to make a special trip to Tianjin to dredge coal transportation. I hope that your chamber of commerce will take into account the difficulties faced by the national industry, commerce, and labor and provide substantial assistance as soon as possible. Benefiting the national economy and people's livelihood will be immeasurable. Correspondingly send a letter, and please check and contact. Sincerely, Lin Kanghou, National Chamber of Commerce Federation of the Republic of China, Wang Xiaolai, National Federation of Industrial Associations, to the Tianjin Chamber of Commerce.

Municipal Chamber of Commerce Asks for Exemption from Increased Freight Rates for Shanxi Coal on the Ping-Sui Railway 89

To Relieve the Coal Shortage Between Tianjin and Shanghai

The Municipal Chamber of Commerce telegraphed the Ministry of Railways yesterday, saying: Nanjing Ministry of Railways, may your Majesty be informed that on the 8th of this month, we received a letter from the Coal Industry Federation of Kou Dong Station on the Ping-Sui Railway, stating that the coal reserves of the Datong Coalfield in Shanxi are the richest in the world, and the coal quality is excellent. It is especially famous at home and abroad for its use in industrial boats. However, because it is located in the hinterland, it is restricted by the expensive freight rates on the Ping-Sui Railway and it is difficult to export. The northern part of Shanxi has always been a poor area that has suffered from wars and droughts and is unable to make a living. The only way to provide relief is to open up coal mines on a large scale so that they can be sold smoothly at home and abroad, so that the people can be relieved. Therefore, the Taiyuan General Chamber of Commerce proposed to reduce the freight rates on the Ping-Sui Railway at the National Business and Transportation Conference in March in order to remedy the situation. Indeed, if Shanxi coal cannot be exported for one day, the livelihoods of the Shanxi people will not be stable for one day. At that time, the masses were leading the way and said that the National Government was working hard to deal with the aftermath and would surely care about the difficulties of the merchants and approve the request. The Ping-Sui Railway Bureau recently announced that it had received an order from the Ministry of Railways that, from May 1st, the freight for each ton of coal from Kouquan to Fengtai, which originally cost about six yuan, would be increased by 15%, which is almost seven yuan per ton. Not only did it not show concern, but it also intensified the situation, causing large and small coal mines in northern Shanxi to intend to suspend work, and tens of thousands of workers would lose their jobs. The livelihoods of the Shanxi people are becoming more and more deteriorated. As far as Shanxi Province is concerned, the harm to merchants and the impact on the local area are already unimaginable. At present, it is also the time when Kailuan is experiencing problems. The various ports of Tianjin and Hebei are experiencing coal shortages. People from all walks of life are calling out and running around to maintain the situation and are sparing no effort. The excellent anthracite coal in northern Shanxi is suitable for transporting more at this time to relieve the fuel shortage in various ports and to serve as a backing for recovering foreign capital and operating the Kailuan coal mine. It is possible to meet the expectations of the late Premier's industry to save the country and to comfort the dying merchants and people. Moreover, state-owned railways were originally intended to develop transportation, open up industry, encourage domestic products, and support trade as prerequisites. Anything related to people's livelihood and maintaining foreign trade should be assisted and encouraged to cultivate its foundation in order to be in line with the main purpose of state-owned enterprises. Today, it is acting arbitrarily, only seeking the meager profits of the railway's current income, and causing endless harm to all parties. As a result, both sides will inevitably suffer losses and all goods will be suspended. The railway bureau's income will inevitably be greatly reduced as a result. Fellow merchants, as merchants, could not fathom the purpose of this price increase. In addition to telegraphing the Ministry of Railways and the Ping-Sui Railway Bureau and Shanxi Provincial Government Chairman Shang separately, please implore you to take back the order to increase prices again, and respectfully send a detailed letter, respectfully requesting your strong assistance and to appeal on our behalf, etc. The same day, we also received a telegram from the Datong County Chamber of Commerce in Shanxi with the same information. Although the various roads have increased freight rates across the board due to high metal prices, Shanxi coal is the only source of profit in the province. At this time, when the war has just ended, the province is in a state of disrepair. If the coal mines are suspended due to high prices and slow sales, tens of thousands more miners will lose their jobs, which will cause even more damage to the local area. Moreover, at a time when the source of Kailuan coal is scarce, from Tianjin in the north to Shanghai in the south, they are all suffering from coal shortages and are planning to dredge the domestic coal transportation to provide relief. If freight rates are increased again and the source of coal supply is blocked, not only will it cause great hidden worries for Shanxi Province, but it will also lead to industrial panic in Tianjin and Shanghai. Therefore, even if freight rates are increased across the board, domestic mine coal should be excluded. I dare to express my feelings and earnestly request that the Ministry of Railways examine and approve it and order the Ping-Sui Railway Bureau to handle the freight for Shanxi coal according to the old regulations in order to maintain it and relieve the business difficulties. It is a public convenience. The Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce respectfully submits.
