Yarn and Cotton 173

The Yarn Market Continues to be Good

The yarn market is firm because overseas cotton yarn conditions are consistently rising. People's sentiment is relatively good, and actual sales are becoming more active. The political situation is easing, rumors are calming down, and buyers' attitude is strong and bullish. Some large merchants have a very good outlook and have no intention of letting go. However, the majority of retail investors have heavy inventories and the political situation is still turbid. In addition, the season is currently slow, and their intention to sell short is also strong. However, the world cotton industry is gradually showing a turnaround. In the afternoon, the market was closed for half a day due to the May 9th Commemoration, it is said.

Bidding is Consistently Upward. At the opening of the previous market, the market atmosphere was firm. The good sentiment due to the rising price of American cotton of grade three, and the buying interest was strong. Each month rose 8 or 9 qian. The closing price was slightly lower, but the result was that each rose 3, 5, 6, or 8 qian. The trading volume totaled 13,400 bales. The market was closed for half a day in the afternoon. Check that Douchu bought Yiyu 1,000 bales, Yichang 600 bales, Senkang 400 bales, Changji 500 bales, Taixing 400 bales, Rongxing 300 bales, and Tongyu 350 bales, Shenxin 300 bales. Xiesheng bought 600 bales, Yicheng 550 bales, Yida 400 bales, Yilong 400 bales, Tianlong 700 bales, Dafeng 400 bales, and Lichang 400 bales. The closing price is recorded on the left,

The Cotton Market Rises 174

American Cotton Gradually Rises ... Inventories are not Abundant

The cotton market has skyrocketed, sentiment is good, and Japanese merchants are holding firm and not letting go. Local inventories are relatively short, so the market atmosphere is getting tighter. There are not a few who sell short and then buy to cover. But spot cotton transactions are still sluggish, so some are selling short. However, the inventory in Hankou is also dry, and American cotton is also rising, so there is a deep fear that it will be difficult to fall, it is said.

Han Standard Rises Two or Three Qian. At the opening of the previous market, the market atmosphere was firm due to the rising price of American cotton again. Each month rose one, two, or three qian. The trading volume totaled 35,600 dan. The market was closed in the afternoon. Check that Yiyu sold 1,600 dan, Shenchang 1,400 dan, Gengfeng 1,600 dan, Hengyi 1,100 dan, and Xinheng 1,500 dan. American Cotton Rebounded Upward Last Week 176

Cold and Rainy in the South ... Short Covering, Colleagues Slightly Entered

New York, 8th, telegram report of the cotton market last week. The rebound of the cotton market last week was due to the cold and rain in the South during the past week. However, the power of its rebound was limited to short covering. Colleagues also slightly bought in, but because the weight of securities is downstream, even though the weather is not good, it has still not significantly increased demand. The sale of fertilizer in the 13 states of the South, from December to April, the past five , decreased by 28.6% compared to the same time last year. The cotton crop report stated that the climate was humid and the temperature was too low, causing the benefits to be delayed. Most are in urgent need of dry and warm weather. The chairman of the Agricultural Policy Bureau, Mr. Stone, said that private estimates of reduced cotton fields averaged 12.5%. This estimate may not be wrong, and the reduction in fertilizer demand can actually prove it. The weekend statistics are attached below. (Unit: 1,000 bales)

Food 178

Customer Xian Rice is Stagnant

Yesterday, the customer Xian rice market was quite quiet. Because the local street had Do-Mi rice coming in continuously, there were no more inquiries. There were also no transactions by customer gangs, and the market was immediately dull. However, the cargo owners were unwilling to reduce prices for sale because the source was cut off, so transactions completely stopped. However, Nanjing rice came by train, without export permits. Furthermore, the cargo could not be stored for long. The cargo owners mostly sought to sell quickly. Yesterday, 424 bags of newly arrived Nanjing machine rice were offered, priced at 9 yuan, 7 jiao and a half to 9 yuan, 7 jiao. Nanjing rice, 500 bags, priced at 8 yuan, 4 jiao to 8 yuan, 2 fen and a half. The price was slightly better than the price offered last month, but weaker than the previous market. It was all taken in by the local street, it is said.

Forward Delivery Flour Houses Absorbing 179

Early Closing of the Trading Session

Yesterday in the flour market, after the opening bell in the morning, foreign wheat prices were quoted up 12 cents, and short covering activity arose to offset losses. Though local buyers did not inquire much, flour houses with forward deliveries were absorbing (flour). Manufacturers were still not selling, and the market price was seen to rise step by step. However, the miscellaneous grains exchange was closed for the day, and there were few buyers at the flour exchange, so there was little trading throughout the day, and the closing of the session was also early. As a result, the current month remained unchanged, June to August were up 5%, September was up 7.5%, and October was up 1%, it is said.

Sugar Market 180

60,000 Bags of Forward Japanese Sugar Opened

Yesterday, sugar market reports from the production areas indicated that Cuban spot sugar prices rose slightly by 0.03125 compared to previous telegrams. New York sugar futures for May rose by one cent, and the remaining months each rose by two cents. Spot Java sugar futures still lacked increases or decreases. In the syndicate market, the buying interest in Dutch sugar No. 24 coarse sand was particularly sluggish, with a quoted price of taels 10.05, and no inquiries at all. There were also few buyers for No. 20 medium white sand at taels 10. Spot Japanese sugar saw some scattered transactions, and the market price remained unchanged. N Mark was still at taels 10.06, YT Mark at taels 10.05, YP Mark at taels 10.0925 to taels 10.09, YRO Mark at taels 9.95, SH Mark at taels 10.015, and J Mark at taels 10.0975. The market shape was still stable. Meiji Sugar opened 30,000 bags for delivery in July and August, including 10,000 bags of YP Mark at a price of Japanese yen 4.50, 14,000 bags of YT Mark at a price of yen 4.435, and 6,000 bags of YRO Mark at a price of yen 3.95. Most of these were purchased by various firms from Zhenjiang, and other businesses showed little interest, so the market atmosphere felt particularly calm and unsurprising. Yu Yuanlai & Co. offered over a hundred bags of No. 3 Ice at taels 13.20, a particularly favorable price. However, the goods were old stock and of inferior color, so there were not many buyers, it is said.

Silk and Tea 181

Foreign Firms' Silk Market Remains Weak

Continuing from this port, the foreign firms' silk market remains weak. The reason is that overseas silk sales are not moving, and telegrams are sparse. Furthermore, the exchange rate is increasing, and the telegrammed silk price is even lower, making transactions difficult. In the past three days, only Jardine Matheson & Co. and others imported fifty bales of Shanghai white factory silk and forty bales of Sichuan yellow factory silk, while Butterfield & Swire and others imported twenty bales of white "qian" silk, and Samsung and others imported twenty-five bales of yellow coarse silk. The price is increasingly weak, it is said.

Spreading of Leaking Yellow and Dead Silkworms Discovered in Wujin Spring Silkworms 182

The current situation of sericulture in the north and south markets and villages of Wujin is not good. The early silkworms in the southwest villages suffered significant losses due to the cold weather. Many in the eastern villages are raising improved varieties, but the weather is unpredictably cold and warm, coupled with continuous spring rains, resulting in unfavorable development of the silkworm larvae. The early silkworms in the western villages have completed their second molt and have sufficient leaves, and the late groups in this area have also completed their second molt. Unexpectedly, continuous heavy rains have caused silkworm diseases to spread, with leaking yellow and dead silkworm diseases being discovered. Silkworm farmers are filled with pessimism, it is said.

Spring Silkworms in Haining Damaged by Heavy Rains 183

Sericulture in the four villages of Haining is unfavorable this spring. Most of the early silkworms were abandoned in the cold rain, and the late silkworms are also developing slowly due to the cold weather, combined with little sunshine and much rain. The heavy rain of the day before yesterday, lasting for two days and nights, caused the silkworm larvae to change. Silkworms that had completed their third molt and had sufficient leaves did not molt and died, and vigorous silkworms were found to be leaking yellow. It is predicted that sericulture this year will inevitably decline, it is said.

The Tea Season in Tunxi is Relatively Good 184

Tunxi is the center of the tea industry in southern Anhui. Due to unfavorable business in recent years, various tea firms have been quite disheartened, either reducing their scope or ceasing operations, and the market situation has been unusually bleak. However, since the beginning of this [month], tea merchants, in view of the low inventory in Shanghai, have once again reorganized and started business one after another. Tea firms have been established one after another, and there are currently as many as forty-six. On the mountain side, due to the difficulty in selling raw tea last year, many have also advanced the picking schedule. Although the weather is cold and the tea buds are not easy to develop, all have entered the mountains to pick green tea on the 5th of this month. It is predicted that the color and quality of tea from this route this year will be superior to previous years, it is said.

Yesterday's News After the New Tea Marketed 185

Yesterday was the second day of the new tea being marketed. The tea factories only had over a hundred boxes on display. They were completely bought by firms such as Jilong, Xiehe, and Tongfu at a price of around taels 100, and the market situation was quite lively. Tea factories such as Yitongxing and Rusheng are employing workers day and night to rush production. Next Monday, a large quantity of "Zhen Mei" new samples will be displayed, it is said.

The Tea Market in Xiushui is Bleak 186

The black tea from Xiushui used to be of superior quality and taste, and was sold to foreign firms in large quantities. In recent years, due to changes in soil and climate, and lack of diligent planting by mountain farmers, the quality of production has deteriorated. The Wuyue and Yingkou groups, which export boxed tea to foreign firms, have suffered repeated losses. The number of firms is decreasing. This year, the number of foreign tea merchants entering the mountains is even rarer than hen's teeth. Only one Wuyue firm continues to operate for foreign firms, and the rest are small organizations operating both tea shops and bamboo-basket tea. New tea from Ruoxi, Kengchi, Manjiang, and Xinchang began to be picked after Guyu [Grain Rain]. The initial mountain price was from 600 to 300-400 cash per catty, similar to last year, but sales to foreign firms have stopped completely, and it all depends on the sales of shop tea. However, the capacity is not very large, and the mountain price must be reduced to allow for large-scale purchases, it is said.

Piece Goods 187

The White Crepe Cloth Market is Improving

Yesterday, in the piece goods market, because the price of "Three Products" rose again and was more firm, the white crepe cloth, which had been weak for a long time, also rose with it. In fact, the price has been gradually increasing, and merchants are optimistic and reluctant to sell. Furthermore, market participants are buying in, so the prices of various brands have risen by about five cents. Yesterday, Moganshan, Jiaoye, and Tishu were all at taels 4.10, Maxie at taels 4.075, Tongpan at taels 4.20. Spot goods are gradually becoming scarce, but "Yuanyang Miao" still lacks vitality and seems to be in a slump. The reason is that Shanghai is full of inventory, and there are many who urgently need to pledge silver, so it is difficult to improve. Yesterday, "Dian Qiuxiang" was still at taels 10.0325, and "Yipin Fugui" spot goods had fallen to taels 10.015. "Little Beauty" has also fallen. The situation requires a period of smooth actual sales before it can turn around. Poplin is still selling well, and fine wool flannel is still actively being traded by the Changjiang group, with over fifty pieces being transacted. "Gongsun Tu" was at cash 0.02925, "Hele Tu" at cash 0.02975, "Ronghua Fugui" at cash 0.03, "Huxin Ting" at cash 0.03275, and "Sanyou Tu" at cash 0.03175, it is said.

Oil Market 188

Tung Oil Prices in Hankou Rise Repeatedly

The reason why White Tung Oil prices in Hankou are repeatedly rising is that during the past week, the foreign firms only traded fractional lots and no integral lots, and happened to be at the time when five to six thousand piculs of Xiang Tung Oil were arriving. This oil was sold as soon as it arrived in Hankou. Therefore, the market was slightly weak as a result. The foreign firms sold the oil for taels 20.04, taels 20.02, taels 20.00, and taels 19.80. Each time the opening session traded only several dozen tons, which wasn't enough to attract the attention of the market. However, the inventory in Hankou is extremely thin, and the dealers who sold short haven't been able to cover their positions. Therefore, it's easiest for the market price to rise as soon as foreign firms trade a large number of lots. Yesterday, this port suddenly received a telegram from Hankou saying that foreign firms had sold at taels 20.08. There were even rumors that another telegram said that it had traded at taels 21.40. Although there's no way to confirm it, it's likely not groundless. As such, it's already risen taels 1.5-1.6 compared to last week. One wouldn't call this a clap of thunder out of the blue. Although we haven't received an official report on the cause of the rise, it's generally due to the fact that overseas sales are flourishing, and the demand has surpassed the supply. Hangzhou also followed suit. According to the firms in Hangzhou, they require thirty-one yuan per picul delivered to Shanghai, which is one yuan higher than before. This port is currently in the midst of the sericulture season in the surrounding areas, so the market can't be as lively as it was half a month ago. Therefore, it can only follow Hankou's lead, it is said.
